# <a name="obsolete-members-in-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="704e6-102">.NET Framework'de eski üyeler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="704e6-102">Obsolete members in .NET Framework</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="704e6-103">Bu makalede, .NET Framework 4.5 ve sonraki sürümlerde eskimiş tür üyeleri listelenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="704e6-103">This article list the type members that are obsolete in .NET Framework 4.5 and later versions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="704e6-104">Tür üyeleri montaja göre gruplandırılır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="704e6-104">Type members are grouped by assembly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="704e6-105">Bu makalede, eski türlerin üyeleri listelemiyor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="704e6-105">This article doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="704e6-106">Eski türlerin listesi için Eski [türleri'ne](obsolete-types.md)bakın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="704e6-106">For a list of obsolete types, see [Obsolete types](obsolete-types.md).</span></span>
